JSON.parse(item) : initialValue;\n    } catch (error) {\n      // If error also return initialValue\n      console.log(error);\n      return initialValue;\n    }\n  });\n\n  // Being repeatedly used in components that is being shown multiple times in a page makes this operation overlaps and causes innacurate updates.\n  // Return a wrapped version of useState's setter function that ...\n  // ... persists the new value to localStorage.\n  const setValue = (value: T | ((val: T) => T)) => {\n    try {\n      // Allow value to be a function so we have the same API as useState\n      const valueToStore =\n        value instanceof Function ? value(storedValue) : value;\n\n      // Save to local storage\n      if (typeof window !== \"undefined\") {\n        try {\n          const serializedValue = JSON.stringify(valueToStore);\n          // in order to fix the overlapping issue, we have\n\n          localStorage.setItem(key, serializedValue);\n          console.log(`✅ Successfully saved to localStorage: ${key}`);\n        } catch (storageError) {\n          if (\n            storageError instanceof DOMException &&\n            storageError.name === \"QuotaExceededError\"\n          ) {\n            console.error(`❌ localStorage quota exceeded for key: ${key}`);\n          } else {\n            console.error(\n              `❌ Failed to serialize/save to localStorage for key: ${key}`,\n              storageError\n            );\n          }\n          // Don't update state if localStorage save failed\n          return;\n        }\n      } else {\n        console.warn(\"⚠️ Cannot save to localStorage: running on server-side\");\n        // Still update state even if we can't persist\n      }\n\n      // Save state only after };\n\n  // this function will only updates and merge values given in the parameter to the correspondinng item inside the current localStorage, and thus preventing overlapping updates between components\n  const updateValue = <T>(value: T | ((val: T) => T)) => {\n    // Get from local storage by key\n    const currentLocalStorageData = localStorage.getItem(key);\n\n    if Merge the new value with the existing data\n        const updatedData = { ...parsedData, ...newValue };\n\n        // Save the updated data back to local storage\n        localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify(updatedData));\n        setStoredValue(updatedData);\n      } catch (error) {\n        console.error(\n          `❌ Failed to update localStorage for key: ${key}`,\n          error\n        );\n      }\n    }\n  };\n\n  return [storedValue, setValue, updateValue];\n}\n/**\n * Practice Statistics Utilities\n * Functions for managing practice statistics in localStorage\n */\n\nimport Via the `providerOptions.openrouter` property:\n\n   ```typescript\n   import { createOpenRouter } from '@openrouter/ai-sdk-provider';\n   import { streamText } from 'ai';\n\n   const openrouter = createOpenRouter({ apiKey: 'your-api-key' });\n   const model = openrouter('anthropic/claude-3.7-sonnet:thinking');\n   await streamText({\n     model,\n     messages: [{ role: 'user', content: 'Hello' }],\n     providerOptions: {\n       openrouter: {\n         reasoning: {\n           max_tokens: 10,\n         },\n       },\n     },\n   });\n   ```\n\n2. Via the `extraBody` property in the model settings:\n\n   ```typescript\n   import { createOpenRouter } from '@openrouter/ai-sdk-provider';\n   import { streamText } from 'ai';\n\n   const openrouter = createOpenRouter({ apiKey: 'your-api-key' });\n   const model = openrouter('anthropic/claude-3.7-sonnet:thinking', {\n     extraBody: {\n       reasoning: {\n         max_tokens: 10,\n       },\n     },\n   });\n   await streamText({\n     model,\n     messages: [{ role: 'user', content: 'Hello' }],\n   });\n   ```\n\n3. The OpenRouter provider will automatically convert these messages to the correct format internally.\n\n### Basic Usage\n\n```typescript\nimport { createOpenRouter } from '@openrouter/ai-sdk-provider';\nimport { streamText } from 'ai';\n\nconst openrouter = createOpenRouter({ apiKey: 'your-api-key' });\nconst model = openrouter('anthropic/<supported-caching-model>');\n\nawait streamText({\n  model,\n  messages: [\n    {\n      role: 'system',\n      content:\n        'You are a podcast summary assistant. You are detail-oriented and critical about the content.',\n    },\n    {\n      role: 'user',\n      content: [\n        {\n          type: 'text',\n          text: 'Given the text body below:',\n        },\n        {\n          type: 'text',\n          text: `<LARGE BODY OF TEXT>`,\n          providerOptions: {\n            openrouter: {\n              cacheControl: { type: 'ephemeral' },\n            },\n          },\n        },\n        {\n          type: 'text',\n          text: 'List the speakers?',\n        },\n      ],\n    },\n  ],\n});\n```\n\n## Use Cases\n\n### Usage Accounting\n\nThe provider supports [OpenRouter usage accounting](https://openrouter.ai/docs/use-cases/usage-accounting), which allows you to track token usage details directly in your API responses, without making additional API calls.\n\n```typescript\n// Enable usage accounting\nconst model = openrouter('openai/gpt-3.5-turbo', {\n  usage: {\n    include: true,\n  },\n});\n\n// Access usage accounting data\nconst result = await generateText({\n  model,\n  prompt: 'Hello, how are you today?',\n});\n\n// Provider-specific usage details (available in providerMetadata)\nif (result.providerMetadata?.openrouter?.usage) {\n  console.log('Cost:', result.providerMetadata.openrouter.usage.cost);\n  console.log(\n    'Total Tokens:',\n    result.providerMetadata.openrouter.usage.totalTokens,\n  );\n}\n```\n- 'enum': The output is an enum.\n- 'no-schema': The output is not a schema.\n\n@param experimental_repairText - A function that attempts to repair the raw output of the model\nto enable JSON parsing.\n\n@param experimental_telemetry - Optional telemetry configuration (experimental).\n\n@param providerOptions - Additional provider-specific options. shuffleArray = (array: VocabularyWord[]): VocabularyWord[] => {\n  const shuffled = [...array];\n  for (let i = shuffled.length - 1; i > 0; i--) {\n    const j = Math.floor(Math.random() * (i + 1));\n filtered.filter((vocab) => !learntVocabs.includes(vocab.word));\n  }\n\n  // Shuffle if requested\n  if (shouldShuffle) {\n    filtered = shuffleArray(filtered);\n  }\n\n  return
